 puranic kathaon ke mutabik, jyeshtha maheene main shanivaar kii amavasya ke din surya kii patni chaaya ne putr ko janm diya, jinka naam shani rakhaa gaya

 surya ko apni is galati kaa ehsaas hua, lekin tab tak bahut der ho gai thi or iskaa parinaam surya ko turant bhugatna padaa
 The sight of his son Shani was blurred and the eclipse of the Sun started
 kehete hai tab se shani kaa rang hameshaa ke liye kaala ho gaya

 kehete hai ki yah kahani shani maharaj ke gussell swabhaav se judi hui he, kaha jaataa he ki shani jab balak the, to ek din unhone apni maa chaaya se bhojan maanga
 He kicked the shadow in anger when there was a delay in getting food

 Women of the third category were asked to do normal dieting, under which they had to eat 1500 calories per day, seven days a week and avoid fatty foods

 According to the exclusive information received by Aaj Tak, Railway Minister Prabhu expressed concern over the frequent train accidents and warned the officers in clear terms that if you are not handling the work then tell it
 railway afasaron ko railmantri ne kaha ki wo apane aaramdaayak daftaron se baahar nikalakar agle saat dinon tak railway sefti se jude tamaam pahaluon kii jaanch-parakh karen
 Along with this, it was also decided in the meeting that for the next 10 days, a senior officer in all the Mail Express trains running across the country will take care of safety by staying on the footplate
